<p
class="title">about</p>









<p
class="bio">
Synonymous
with
Bay
Area
rap,
E-40
garnered
a
regional
following,
and
eventually
a
national
one,
with
his
flamboyant
raps,
while
his
entrepreneurial
spirit,
embodied
by
his
homegrown
record
label,
Sick
Wid'
It
Records,
did
much
to
cultivate
a
flouris...
</p>

href="/e40/bio">read
more</a>
